              "      <script>\n",
              "        const buttonEl =\n",
              "          document.querySelector('#df-40a9d027-82a7-400e-837e-bf4523d7767f button.colab-df-convert');\n",
              "        buttonEl.style.display =\n",
              "          google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed ? 'block' : 'none';\n",
              "\n",
              "        async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "          const element = document.querySelector('#df-40a9d027-82a7-400e-837e-bf4523d7767f');\n",
              "          const dataTable =\n",
              "            await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                     [key], {});\n",
              "          if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "          const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "            '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "            + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "          element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "          dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "          await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "          const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "          docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "          element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "        }\n",
              "      </script>\n",
              "    </div>\n",
              "  </div>\n",

              "        const buttonEl =\n",
              "          document.querySelector('#df-d6b107d9-04e4-45bf-84cd-dd7dae44d791 button.colab-df-convert');\n",
              "        buttonEl.style.display =\n",
              "          google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed ? 'block' : 'none';\n",
              "\n",
              "        async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "          const element = document.querySelector('#df-d6b107d9-04e4-45bf-84cd-dd7dae44d791');\n",
              "          const dataTable =\n",
              "            await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                     [key], {});\n",
              "          if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "          const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "            '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "            + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "          element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "          dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "          await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "          const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "          docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "          element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "        }\n",
              "      </script>\n",
              "    </div>\n",
              "  </div>\n",
              "  "
            ]

        "from keras.models import Sequential\n",
        "from keras.layers import Dense\n",
        "import tensorflow as tf\n",
        "\n",
        "\"\"\"顺序模型：类似于搭积木一样一层、一层放上去\"\"\"\n",
        "# 用Sequential建立模型\n",
        "model = tf.keras.Sequential()\n",
        "\n",
        "\n",
        "\"\"\"添加层:其实就是 wx+b\"\"\"\n",
        "model.add(tf.keras.layers.Dense(units=50, activation='relu', input_dim=3))\n",
        "# model.add(tf.keras.layers.Dropout(0.2))\n",
        "# model.add(tf.keras.layers.Dense(units=150, activation='relu'))\n",
        "# model.add(tf.keras.layers.Dropout(0.2))\n",

        "# model.add(tf.keras.layers.Dense(units=50, activation='relu'))\n",
        "model.add(tf.keras.layers.Dense(units=25, activation='relu'))\n",
        "model.add(tf.keras.layers.Dense(units=10, activation='relu'))\n",
        "model.add(tf.keras.layers.Dense(units=2, activation='softmax'))\n",
        "\n",
        "\n",
        "\n",
        "\n",
        "#編譯模型\n",
        "model.compile(loss='categorical_crossentropy', optimizer='adam', metrics=['accuracy'])\n",
        "\n",
        "\n",
        "# 顯示模型\n",
        "tf.keras.utils.plot_model(model,show_shapes=True)\n",
        "\n",
        "#===================================================================\n",
        "\n",
        "\"\"\"编译，配置\"\"\"\n",
        "# model每層定義好後需要經過compile\n",
        "# optimizer最佳化工具為adam\n",
        "# 方法為keras.losses.mean_squared_error\n",
        "\n",
        "model.compile(optimizer= 'adam',\n",
        "               loss=['categorical_crossentropy'],\n",
        "               metrics=['accuracy']\n",
        "                  )\n",
        "# 多分類loss函數:categorical_crossentropy\n",
        "# 二分類loss函數:binary_crossentropy\n",
        "\n",

        "# val_accuracy\n",
        "\n",
